dividend increase, raising the quarterly dividend 15% from&#160;$1.01 to $1.16&#160;per share of common stock, payable on&#160;December 17, 2018&#160;to shareholders of record at the close of business on&#160;December 3, 2018. This brings the fourth quarter dividend payout to nearly&#160;$900 million. McDonald&#8217;s has experienced increased capital allocation flexibility due to the evolution of the Company&#8217;s business model and the effects of the Tax Cuts and Jobs Act of 2017.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:11pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">McDonald's&#160;President and Chief Executive Officer&#160;Steve Easterbrook&#160;said, "Our substantial cash flow enables us to invest in the business to drive growth under our Velocity Growth Plan.
